Various Trade Associations Convene to Discuss the Implementation Rules of the Trade Association Law

▲ Telegram to the Central Government to Stop Trade Union Activities

▲ Telegram to the Central Government to Re-amend the Trade Association Law

The various trade associations in this city convened a meeting of representatives from various industries yesterday afternoon in the auditorium of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to discuss various issues after the revision of the implementation rules of the Trade Association Law. Representatives from over eighty groups, including the Flour Industry, Cigarette Industry, Knitting Industry, New Medicine Industry, Seafood and Grocery Industry, Brick and Tile Industry, Pollen Industry, Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry, Sausage Industry, North and South Goods Industry, and Tea and Food Industry, as well as Chu Wen-chi, Sun Ching-tien, Shen Wei-ting, Cheng Hai-jo, Shao Pao-hsing, Chen Tzu-hsiang, Cheng Cheng-ching, Yeh Chia-hsing, and Sun Chou-cheng, a total of over one hundred people, elected Deng Cheng-qing as chairman and Xue Guang-qian as recorder. After the ceremonial proceedings, Chairman Deng Cheng-qing reported that the main purpose of convening the meeting was to discuss various issues after the central government abolished trade unions and revised the implementation rules of the Trade Association Law. This issue not only concerns the status of the various trade associations themselves but also has a significant impact on the inherent social system and economic organization. At the Third National Congress in 1929, in order to ensure that the mass movement met the needs of the tutelage period, separate principles were established and a plan for organizing people's organizations was formulated, dividing people's organizations into professional organizations and social organizations, with the exception of local self-government organizations that were regulated otherwise. The former included trade unions, farmers' associations, chambers of commerce, trade associations, etc., and the latter included student, women's, cultural, and religious groups. Each type of organization has its own specific laws and regulations. Trade unions have the Trade Union Law, chambers of commerce have the Chamber of Commerce Law, and trade associations have the Trade Association Law. Store clerk trade unions are not included in professional organizations, thus losing their legal footing and being virtually eliminated because the central government believes that store clerks are auxiliary to the main commercial entity and engage in commerce as commercial employees under commercial law. Their nature is the same as that of store owners, so there is no need to organize separately, which would create a confrontational situation with trade associations. Past facts have made this clear. Although the organization of trade unions has been nominally abolished, there is still the opportunity to participate in organizations. Article 10 of the implementation rules of the Trade Association Law stipulates that "each company or firm may send one to two member representatives as managers or main persons in charge. However, if the average number of store clerks in the most recent year is more than fifteen, one additional representative may be sent, elected by the store clerks of the respective company or firm." Therefore, store clerks also have the opportunity to participate in trade associations. However, the central government has recently made major revisions to this clause. The main points are as follows: (1) The number of store clerks required to send an additional representative has been reduced from fifteen to ten or more; (2) Store clerks may send up to three additional representatives, while store owners may only send one or two representatives; (3) The phrase "may" has been changed to "shall" in the legal text. "May" is an arbitrary provision, while "shall" has a mandatory nature. Considering the above three points, the organization of trade associations will be fundamentally shaken because the commerce in this city is relatively prosperous, and the number of employees used is generally not small. The number of stores with thirty or forty or more store clerks is numerous. According to the revised provisions, store clerks can send three representatives, but store owners can send a maximum of two representatives. Is such an association, organized with such a composition (three to two), still a trade association of the same trade, or will it become a trade association of store clerks? This is a very big question because store owners are busy planning and managing their businesses and are busy all day long. It is undeniable that they lack training and attention to groups. Therefore, the center of gravity of the association will inevitably be tied to the store clerks. It is obvious whether such an association will seek benefits for store owners or focus solely on the interests of store clerks. Judging from this situation, those who have not previously organized will not want to or dare to organize again. Those who have already organized would rather dissolve because allowing them to exist is like "lifting a rock only to drop it on one's own feet," providing an additional layer of protection and exploitation for store clerks. Looking at the future of trade associations in this way, how can we not shudder? The purpose of convening you all here today is to discuss this urgent issue of the life and death of trade associations. We should strive with the central government to request a re-amendment. All of you are prominent figures in the business community, and I hope you will all share your opinions. What I have reported is merely the limited perspective of a fool, hoping to elicit valuable insights. The discussion followed, and the resolutions were as follows: (1) Telegram to the central government to stop trade union activities and legally join trade associations; (2) Telegram to the central government that the implementation rules of the Trade Association Law should be re-amended, and that the number of store clerk representatives should be one for every ten or more people and should not exceed two. The above resolutions were forwarded to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the meeting adjourned.

Methods for Store Clerks to Join Trade Associations

▲ Should First Withdraw from the Trade Union

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a report to the Social Affairs Bureau regarding a petition. On March 2, the Duck Slaughtering Trade Association sent a letter stating that it had previously received a letter from the Chamber of Commerce asking for clarification on whether duck slaughterers who solicit customers after slaughtering ducks fall under the scope of "employees." This matter was submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for instructions. Today, the Chamber of Commerce received Instruction No. 6393 from the Social Affairs Bureau, which stated, "We have received the report. It is stated that all workers in the duck slaughtering industry in this city must be qualified in the business, and they naturally fall within the scope of 'employees.' According to the provisions of Article 10 of the recently revised Implementation Rules of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, when the number of employees exceeds ten, one representative should be added, but the maximum number should not exceed three. Please forward this to the relevant parties for compliance." In response, a letter was forwarded, requesting that the matter be handled accordingly and inquiring whether the workers in question had a trade union organization. It stated, "Our trade's partners already have a duck slaughtering trade union organization and have also signed labor-management contracts. Based on previous practices, all members are notified to inform their partners and legally elect representatives to join." The letter went on to state that duck slaughterers already have a trade union organization, and it is different from cases where trade unions cannot legally exist and their members must be merged into trade associations. Now, according to the instructions from your bureau, these workers are directly serving in the business and should be considered within the scope of employees, and they should elect representatives to join the trade association. If these workers have previously joined the duck slaughtering trade union, it seems that they should be ordered to withdraw from the duck slaughtering trade union before joining the trade association to clarify the boundaries and avoid one person joining two types of organizations, which would undermine the independence of the organization. Is this appropriate? We hereby submit this to your bureau for review and instructions for compliance.

The Kai Li Shipping Company to Open Coastal Routes in Eastern Zhejiang

▲ Sailings to Commence Tomorrow

▲ The primary reason for the establishment is that shipping expert Bao Da-ting, recognizing the large volume of goods transported from various coasts of Eastern Zhejiang to Shanghai, which were usually transported by multiple transshipments without dedicated steamships, resulting in high costs and long times, decided to establish coastal shipping lines in Eastern Zhejiang to facilitate merchants and passengers. He first consulted with Shen Liang-cheng and others, proposing a capital of 500,000 yuan to purchase steamships for sailings to places such as Shenjiamen. Shen also supported this. The matter was prepared in the autumn of last year and has now been established.

▲ Company Name Since Bao Jin Xing began operations, there have been many domestic investors. Qiu Zuo-yin has also joined, and is in charge of the economic aspect, while Shen Liang-cheng has withdrawn from the company. It is named Kai Li Shipping Company, with an initial capital of 100,000 yuan. The head office is located on Guangdong Road in Shanghai, and a 1,000-ton Japanese steamship was purchased from Jenson & Co. for over 50,000 yuan and heavily renovated by Huaxin Chang to add passenger berths. It was only completed yesterday. This ship has an extremely high speed and can travel 11 nautical miles per hour.

▲ Navigation Routes The navigation routes have been determined and divided into long and short routes. A short route will depart every Monday, going from Shanghai to Shengshan, Sijiao, Daishan, Gaoting, Putuo, and Shenjiamen. The long route, on Thursdays, will go from Shanghai to Putuo, Guoji, Hengshan, Wuyu Mountain, Xiangshan, Xizhou, Xiashan, and Xueao (i.e., Xueao). The ship is named Kai Yuan, and the maiden voyage is scheduled for tomorrow. The Shanghai pier is located at Dada Pier No. 3.

▲ Fare Prices Set The company has set the fare prices for various places yesterday. We are reporting them as follows:

Destination Cabin Fare Steerage Fare

Shengshan 2.6 yuan 2 yuan

Guoji Mountain 3.6 yuan 2 yuan

Dongshajiao Gaoting 2.4 yuan 1.2 yuan

Guoji Wuyu Mountain 3 yuan 1.6 yuan

Huanglong 3.6 yuan 2 yuan

Sijiao 3.6 yuan 2 yuan

Putuo Shenjiamen 2.4 yuan 1.2 yuan

Baidun Xizhou Xiashan Xueao 3 yuan 1.6 yuan

Chongsha Shipping Competition Fails

▲ Six Companies Alliance Cooperation

▲ Today's Meeting to Form Trade Association

▲ Implementing Reduced Sailings and Increased Passenger Fares

With the rise of gold prices, the shipping industry has experienced extreme panic, either raising freight rates or seeking alliances. Since March, various shipping companies have been seeking remedial measures. The previous trend of price competition has vanished and disappeared, replaced by efforts to increase revenue. Due to business relationships, the various shipping companies on the Shanghai-Chongsha route have been experiencing fierce competition since last year. Over the past year, the companies have suffered huge losses. Now, under the impact of high gold prices and low silver prices, they are almost unable to sustain themselves and have to try to salvage the situation. They have abandoned the competition and are cooperating in an alliance. The details are reported as follows:

▲ Competing on the Chongsha Route There are six Shanghai-based merchant ships operating on the Shanghai-Chongsha route: Daxing, Pingan, Jufeng, Dada, Baoji, and Xinxinglong, with six ships, including Fuxing, Baohua, Haimen, and Xinxingda, sailing the route. The route is from Shanghai to Chongming and Haimen. The number of daily sailings has increased to four. The main goods coming from Chongsha are cotton and homespun cloth, while the goods going to Chongsha are North-South goods and foreign miscellaneous goods. With fewer ports of call and a limited number of goods and passengers, the six companies have been competing with all their might in terms of passengers, abandoning fixed fares and competing by lowering prices.

▲ Losses The majority of passengers traveling to and from Chongsha are steerage passengers. The original fare was 60 cents per person. Since the competition between the six companies began, the fares have been reduced several times, eventually selling for 20 cents per person, a reduction of two-thirds of the original amount. Since last year, with four ships sailing daily, there has been a phenomenon of too many ships and too few goods and passengers on this route. The daily revenue from passenger and freight fares has been insufficient to cover fuel and labor costs. The six companies have suffered significant losses since last year.

▲ Relief In recent months, gold prices have been rising, and material costs have been increasing. The six companies have felt the growing hidden losses in their operations, which are unsustainable. Xu Zhongxin of Daxing and Chen Shutang of Pingan have proposed relief measures, suggesting that the six companies should abandon competition and adopt an open cooperative attitude. Following the example of the Shanghai-Taiwan Six Companies' United Navigation Association, they should also operate in an alliance. Xu and others have sought the consent of various companies and decided to change their previous approach, agreeing to organize a common agency to manage the six shipping companies and adopt a public sharing method to salvage the situation.

▲ Alliance The six companies have drafted representatives to go to the Shipping Trade Association today to begin discussing the alliance cooperation method. The principles that have been drafted are: 1. The six companies will jointly form a unified office to manage all shipping operations; 2. The ship schedules will be allocated by the trade association; 3. The number of daily sailings will be reduced to two; 4. The ticket price will be restored to the original price; 5. The freight revenue will be shared equally according to the tonnage of the ships. The general methods are as such. The detailed rules of the alliance, and the percentage of business shared, must wait until the proposal is made today before they can be decided.

Progress of the New Kang Disaster Relief Association

The New Kang Ship Disaster Relief Association discussed litigation issues yesterday. Standing Committee member Mr. Zhu and legal counsel Sheng Zhenwei, a prominent lawyer, had a lengthy discussion. The results of the discussion were: (1) The various witnesses and material evidence for the lawsuits are complete; (2) The complaints have also been drafted; (3) Regarding the litigation relief issue, it was decided that the Disaster Relief Association would submit a request to the Ministry of Judicial Administration for special assistance; (4) A date will be set to talk to the lawyer representing the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company; (5) A date will be set to convene a plenary committee meeting.

After the Autopsy of Zhang Wenyi's Body

▲ The Body Was Coffined at the Fortress Yesterday

The incident where the body of Zhang Wenyi, the garrison battalion commander of the Wusong Fortress, was privately autopsied by Baolong Hospital has been reported in previous newspapers. The body has been transported back to the fortress in a car and coffined. The family members believe that after Battalion Commander Zhang's death, the hospital dared to autopsy the body without the permission of the family and requested Commander Deng to negotiate with the hospital. Commander Deng approved the transfer of the situation to the Ministry of Military Affairs and Law for strict punishment, in order to warn against illegal acts and maintain humanity. In addition, to commemorate the previous merits of the battalion commander, a memorial service will be held at the fortress on March 9. The adjutant's office has been ordered to prepare everything yesterday.

The Tragic News of Corpses Waiting to Be Buried in Shaanxi

▲ Telegram from the Shaanxi Provincial Disaster Relief Association

Yesterday, the Chinese Red Cross Society received a telegram from the Shaanxi Provincial Disaster Relief Association, reporting that the disaster investigation committee in the western region reported that there were still more than 20,000 corpses unburied in Qian and Mei counties, and the situation was very tragic. The details are disclosed in the following telegram: "To the General Office of the Chinese Red Cross Society and to be forwarded to various charitable organizations and philanthropists: We have received a report from the disaster investigation committee in the western region stating that the disaster is severe in various areas of the western region. Not only are the living freezing and starving to death, but many of the dead have not been buried. Most villages are deserted, and corpses are lying in the rooms, with a foul smell. The tragic situation is hard to describe. For example, there are about 10,000 corpses in Wugong, and there is no way to bury them. Last year, the North China Charity Federation spent more than 10,000 yuan in Qian and Mei counties and only buried over 7,000 corpses. A recent investigation found that there are still more than 20,000 people unburied in these two counties. There are also many unburied in other counties, such as Xingping, Fufeng, and Xianyang. If they are left exposed, not only is it unbearable, but the spring air is gradually warming up, which will inevitably lead to epidemics that will harm the disaster victims who are waiting to die. We want to send personnel to bury them, but there are too many, and we do not have such a large amount of money. We implore you to show compassion and widely appeal to raise funds for the burial, to benefit the dry bones and prevent epidemics. The dead will know and repay the favor, and the living will be spared from the plague and be grateful for your infinite virtue. We hereby appeal to you and ask you to investigate. Shaanxi Provincial Disaster Relief Association, Yang Yin."

News from Trade Associations

▲ South Goods Industry The South Goods Trade Association held a membership luncheon meeting at the Chongyi Hall on Ninghe Road on March 1. More than 180 members attended. Chairman Gong Jingyan reported on business issues, stating that the 0.5% tax rate for the industry violated the general principles because the industry's products are necessities for the people and cannot be compared with other industries. It is not something that businesses can afford. It was resolved to send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Tariff Committee to forward to the central government, requesting that the industry's tax rate not exceed 0.1% and that the tax be collected on a business unit basis. Regarding the issue of increasing commissions in the letter from the Seafood and Grocery Trade Association, it was resolved to send a letter denying all new and old commissions. Regarding the issue of the first bidding period this year, it was resolved to set March 16 as the first bidding period this year. After the discussion, a photo was taken and the meeting adjourned.

▲ Straw Hats Industry The Straw Hats Trade Association held a meeting the day before yesterday afternoon, chaired by Cao Moqing, to discuss various issues: (1) How to increase prices due to excessive costs? It was resolved to set a full price without discounts. (2) Pricing for thick and thin straw hats? Passed, the lowest price. (3) Effective date of the new price list? Resolved, effective from the date of publication in the newspaper. (4) Formulation of trade rules? Passed. (5) How to punish those who violate the agreed prices? Resolved, strict punishment. The meeting adjourned as the streetlights came on at 6 o'clock.

Five Children Infatuated with Wuxia Novels

Planning to go to Mount Emei to Cultivate Taoism

Envious of Many Swordsmen Soaring Through the Clouds and Riding the Mist

Using Tuition Fees as Travel Expenses to Take a Steamer to Sichuan

One Young Child Homesick and Crying Spoils the Undertaking

Five Children Separately Claimed by Their Families

A year ago, three apprentices from a certain tailor shop in the French Concession became obsessed with old novels, so they went together to a certain mountain temple to become monks and practice. They were eventually sent back by the monks of the temple, and it was rumored throughout Shanghai, and everyone regarded it as a strange story. Unexpectedly, recently there were five children, all over ten years old, who were usually fascinated by reading wuxia novels, and actually also planned to go to Sichuan to cultivate Taoism. Eventually they were found by their families, and the matter did not achieve their ambitions. The details are recorded below.

Four Children Infatuated with Wuxia Novels Rent a Residence

Ye Shengchao, a Fujianese lawyer who practices law at No. 82 Jiruili, Jiuda Lane, Gaochang Temple, Nanshi, has two sons. The elder son is named Guangyuan, seventeen years old, and the younger son is named Guangji, fifteen years old. They are both studying at the Guohua School on Baker Road in the Public Concession. They are extremely intelligent. Zheng Baoyuan, a Ningbo native residing at No. 78 Nanlinli, Haining Road, Public Concession, also has two sons, the elder named Jingqing, sixteen years old, and the younger named Jingming, eleven years old. They are classmates with the Ye brothers. In recent years, the wuxia novels published by bookstores have become popular in society, and have a great momentum in the novel world. Guangyuan, Guangji and Jingqing are also part of those who like to read them. In their spare time after class, they often each hold a volume, quite oblivious of eating and sleeping. Although Jingming is young, he is happy and tireless when he hears the three of them talking about the martial arts in the book. Therefore, the four children share the same aspirations and admire the so-called great heroes who roam the world in novels, which exceeds all other aspirations. Moreover, various movie theaters often show martial arts films. The four children have witnessed many swordsmen soaring through the clouds and riding the mist, and using all kinds of martial arts methods and magic weapons. This has made them even more infatuated.

Planning to Go to Sichuan Together to Learn Taoism Last Year

The school was about to have winter vacation. The four children suddenly proposed taking this opportunity to leave their families and choose a temple in a remote mountain forest with excellent scenery to become monks, practice martial arts. Because they heard that the Emei Mountains in Sichuan Province are the birthplace of great swordsmen, and various schools such as Kunlun, Wudang, and Kongtong gather there. However, they are separated by thousands of miles, which is not within the reach of foot strength. Although there are Sichuan steamer ships in Shanghai, it is difficult to raise the money for the boat fare in a short time. Therefore, they planned to obtain tuition fees from their families when they enter school this year, and use them to change them into travel expenses, and take a steamer to Sichuan. After the plan was decided, they did not publicize it. Later, Jingqing pulled a friend to join, to strengthen their resolve. The friend's name is Pan Yiqin, seventeen years old, the son of Pan Yanzhu, an Anhui native who lives at No. 1001, Siwenli, Datong Road, Xinzha.

Five Children Bought Steamer Tickets to Yichang Last Month

On the 22nd, Guangyuan and Guangji, the two brothers, first obtained a total of 230 yuan for tuition and board from their family. Thinking that this money was enough for the five people's travel expenses, they did not wait for Jingqing and others to have money or not, and were anxious to leave. That morning, under the pretext of going to school, they first went to the Andong Hotel at No. 133, Wuma Road, Daxin Street, opened room number 133, and summoned Jingqing, Jingming, and Yiqin, and discussed the steps to go to Sichuan. Later, seeing that there was a person selling steamer tickets in the hotel, they inquired about Sichuan steamers. They learned that the Yichang steamer of the Jiejang Company was departing from Shanghai to Chongqing. The Shanghai port was docked at the Ruitong Iron Factory Wharf in Hudong. The steamer ticket was 30 yuan per person. Five children could buy three steamer tickets in total. Guangyuan and his party thought that Chongqing was an important commercial port in Sichuan. If they arrived there, they would probably not be far from visiting Mount Emei. Therefore, they decided to take the Yichang steamer to Sichuan. They bought three tickets from the ticket seller, totaling 90 yuan, plus food and other expenses of 33 yuan, totaling 123 yuan. They entrusted the person to choose a berth on the steamer on their behalf. The five children stayed in the hotel for two nights, prepared all the luggage they brought, and then took a car to the steamer wharf to board the steamer.

One Child Cries and is Sent Home Unexpectedly

The steamer did not depart for a while. The five children stayed on the steamer for several days. Jingming eventually because of his young age, it was difficult to get rid of the thought of his family. Moreover, except for the four people traveling together, he felt even more uneasy seeing strangers. He cried all the time. The day before yesterday, his brother Jingqing decided to send him home, and he still returned to the steamer. His father, Zheng Baoyuan, had been looking for his two sons for many days. He was overjoyed to see his younger son returning home. After inquiring about the details, he was overjoyed and surprised. In addition to notifying the families of the other three children, he also entrusted Gu Yuenian and Liang Gengshun, two members of the Special Zone Citizens Association, to report to the water patrol police station first. The head of the police station ordered Chinese detective Deng Jiageng to find the four children in the steerage of the steamer, and brought them and their luggage to the police station for disposal.

The Ambition to Cultivate Taoism Suddenly Suffers a Blow

When the five children boarded the steamer, they brought several pieces of luggage, including a suitcase, two sets of bedding, a rattan basket, and a wallet, which contained a boxing diagram, two Shaolin boxing books, and many other martial arts books and wuxia novels. They also brought an alarm clock, a thermos, a Yueqin, and nourishing products such as white fungus and ginseng, and a lot of scattered clothes. After the children arrived at the police station, the head of the police station questioned their names and origins, and found seven silver dollars next to Guangyuan. It is said that the rest had been used up. He then sent Chinese detective Cheng Yongnian to the original hotel to return the ticket price and other expenses. Then the four children were handed over to their respective families to be taken away. Therefore, the five children's ambition to leave home to go to Sichuan to cultivate Taoism was not fulfilled.

The Bandit Involved in Kidnapping Liu Tongyun, Miao Liancheng, is Arrested

▲ Hiding in Taopeng Road, Hongkou

▲ Detectives Secretly Go to Arrest

Liu Tongyun, a wealthy merchant in Shanghai, opened the Fuji Paper Shop in Chunjiangli, Dagou Bridge, Public Concession. Because his business was prosperous, he was coveted by bandits. He was kidnapped by bandits at about 8 pm on September 19 last year. After several negotiations, it was heard that he was redeemed by paying money. However, the police station, because the kidnapping wind in the concession was rampant, was greatly related to public security, so Chinese and foreign detectives were investigating day and night. Yesterday afternoon, Shao Jingfan, the detective of the Gordon Road Police Station, and detectives Wang Youshan and Xu Decheng, received a tip from an informant that the bandit leader who kidnapped Liu Tongyun was now hiding at No. 774 Jichengfang, Taopeng Road, Hongkou. After Shao Detective received the news, he reported to the head of the police station, and together with foreign detectives, prepared weapons, drove a patrol car, and went straight to Hongkou. After connecting to the address to arrest him, he immediately captured the bandit Miao Liancheng, a native of Jiangbei, and also found contraband in his home, and brought him back to the police station. After the head of the police station briefly questioned him, he scheduled him to be sent to the court for trial today.

Female Nun Qing Shan Steals and Excavates the Coffin of Her Seventh-Generation Ancestor

▲ A Thief in the Lujia Guanyintang

▲ Stealing and Selling Two Mu and Six Fen of Land

Lin Gen, the abbess of the Lujia Guanyintang on Changbang Road in the Public Concession, hired a lawyer to write a complaint and filed a criminal lawsuit with the Shanghai Local Court against her rebellious disciple Qing Shan, who colluded with land dealers to steal and sell her ancestral tombs, and at night excavate the coffin of her seventh-generation ancestral master, and discard the bones. The court has approved the petition and ordered a summons for investigation. The details are extracted and recorded below.

Qing Shan is Not Qing Shan. Lujia Guanyintang is the Lu Family Nunnery. It is now presided over by the old nun Lin Gen. There are a total of five nuns. Qing Shan is Lin Gen's disciple, currently forty-four years old. She became a nun halfway through life and lives in the same room with Lin Gen. Later, because Qing Shan did not abide by the precepts and ate opium, she owed a lot of private debts. At the end of last year, she could not repay them, so she stole the land deed and grain string of the tomb to pledge for silver dollars. Later, a land dealer found out and colluded to steal and sell them.

▲ Taking Advantage of the Fire Alarm to Steal the Deed The tomb is located along Hongqiao Road, covering an area of two mu and six fen. There are seven coffins buried (Lin Gen's seventh-generation ancestral master). The land deed was originally hidden by Lin Gen in a leather box in the room. At the beginning of December of the previous year, there was a siren sound outside the nunnery. The nun suspected that there was a fire alarm, took out the land deed and other items, placed them under the pillow, and then went outside to investigate. She learned that it was a theft by a certain family nearby, and she was relieved. However, the land deed was not stored in the box at the time, so it was stolen by the rebellious disciple Qing Shan.

Workers Come to Dig the Coffin After the land deed was stolen, Qing Shan went out and did not return. Until a certain night last month, several workers came to the tomb and excavated all seven coffins buried there, putting all the bones together and taking them away. It is not known where they were thrown. The next day, someone reported to the nunnery. The abbess Lin Gen and her disciples went to see and immediately called the person in charge of the tomb to inquire about the excavation situation. Only then did they learn that it had been stolen and sold by Qing Shan.

Taking Photos to Collect Evidence The old nun took a photographer to the tomb the day before yesterday and took three photos: (1) seven empty coffins dug out of the soil; (2) old boundary stones; (3) tombs that were excavated and destroyed, etc. She prepared to present these photos to the court for inspection when the court summons her. However, the nun has now found that the land guard Ye did not come to the scene to seal the deed when the tomb was stolen and sold, and has found that the bones dug out of the soil have now been buried in a certain public cemetery.

Continued Trial of the Assassin of Zhao Tieqiao

▲ Strict Interrogation of the Instigator

▲ The Court Forbids Public Attendance

The assassins of Zhao Tieqiao, Xia Shaoen, Wang Jishan, and Cheng Haihong, have been prosecuted by the local court. Yesterday morning at 11 o'clock, Judge Zhao opened the court. Xia Shaoen confessed that he was from Hefei, Anhui. In January of the 18th year of the Republic of China, he went to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and was introduced by Ren Shaolan and Xu Cairen. He was a soldier with a monthly salary of fifteen yuan. After ten months, they were all dismissed. I don't know Chief Zhao. Because I was stationed in Yangjiadu, Pudong, he never came. After I was dismissed, I sold vegetables for a living. I didn't hit him. I heard from the detective that if I admitted three halls at the procuratorate, I could be released, otherwise I would be tortured. The official said, you are like an executioner, killing people after receiving instructions from others. You must tell the truth. Who instigated you? The law has different degrees of severity. There is no need to suffer for others. Xia still denied it. Because it was noon, he was ordered to be taken down. In the afternoon, the interrogation continued, because the strict interrogation was related to the instigator, public attendance was forbidden. It is heard that the trial will continue.

▲ About Twenty Years Old

▲ Wearing a Long Robe on the Outside and a Western Suit on the Inside

Next to the Dongyang Garden on Dong Tiyu Road, Jiangwan, at around 7 o'clock yesterday morning, an unnamed male corpse was found, about twenty years old. After receiving the report, the public security bureau of the fifth district dispatched the police to inspect. There seemed to be no obvious injuries on his body. What was different was that it had been raining for the past two days, but there was no mud on the deceased's socks. There was also a faint blue and purple color on his forehead. The office reported to the local court to request an autopsy.

A Laborer Jumps Off a Car to Pick Up a Hat

▲ Dies Miserably with a Broken Head

At around 2 pm the day before yesterday, a truck carrying goods and many laborers was driving from south to north on Henan Road at a very fast speed. At that time, the wind and rain were intensifying, blowing the hat of laborer Yu Yousheng to the ground. Yu wanted to pick up his hat, but without telling the driver to stop, he jumped out of the car, damaging his head. Fresh blood gurgled out, and he died on the way. The patrol officer at the scene reported to the police station, and the police dispatched a detective to the scene and carried the corpse to the Fielun Road autopsy site. It was then found that the deceased was from Ningbo, 22 years old, and lived at No. 7 Xiexingli, Baoxing Road, Zhabei, with his parents. After notifying the deceased's father, Yu Laicheng, he first went to the autopsy site yesterday morning and reported to the Special Court to send Prosecutor Guo to the site for an autopsy. He was instructed to hand over the body to Laicheng to claim the coffin and burial.

According to the Traffic Department of the Public Concession Police Station, the number of traffic accidents in the concession last month decreased slightly compared to January, with a total of 853 cases, 6 deaths, and 240 injuries. It was found that there were a total of 950 cases in January, 8 deaths, and 262 injuries, which were more than in February. However, compared with the same period last year, it has increased by more than 80 cases.

Responsibility Issues in Car Collisions

▲ No Evidence After Investigation

▲ Dong Aru Released on Bail

Dou Jinyuan, the owner of the Xingfa Automobile Company on Disui Road, drove car No. 17846 on the night of the 28th of last month, driven by driver Wang Afu, and drove from south to north to the intersection of Baoding Road and Tangshan Road. At that time, Dong Aru, the driver of the Yunfei Automobile Company in the French Concession, was driving car No. 12342, carrying three daughters, two young children, and passed by the place, from west to east. Then, with a loud bang, the two cars collided. The passengers were severely shaken. Fortunately, the women and children were unharmed. Only Dou Jinyuan was severely injured. The police inquired and found that the accident was caused by Dong Aru, and immediately arrested him and sent Dou to the hospital. Unfortunately, he was severely injured and the treatment was ineffective. He died shortly after. The Special District Local Court was reported, and the prosecutor was appointed to conduct an autopsy. He ordered the corpse to be coffined and buried, and the police station investigated the circumstances of the accident to determine responsibility. However, after investigation, there was no sufficient evidence to determine who was at fault, and it was not easy to determine at the time. Therefore, it was not convenient to detain Dong any further. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Special Court, and the police station lawyer stated that before obtaining conclusive evidence, he requested that Dong Aru be released on bail, and the police station would continue to conduct the investigation. Judge Xiao, because the victim

Datong and Dabe Can Temporarily Transfer Telegrams via Water Line

▲ Chuanshi Mountain and Gulangyu

▲ Only for One Month

Since the borrowing lines of Chuanshi Mountain and Gulangyu in Fuzhou and Xiamen have been recovered, all telegrams sent to Fuzhou, Xiamen, Shantou, Guangzhou and other places are sent by the local Chinese Telegraph Office. It is now learned that the office has recently received an order from the Ministry of Communications, temporarily allowing Datong and Dabe Companies to use water lines to transfer telegrams in Chuanshi Mountain and Gulangyu from March 1 for a period of one month, but they are not allowed to directly receive or send to the public. The right to receive and send is still in the hands of our country's Chuan and Gu Telegraph Offices. Therefore, the right to send telegrams to Fuzhou, Xiamen, Shantou, Guangzhou and other places received by Datong and Dabe Companies in recent days must still be managed by the Chinese Telegraph Offices in Fuzhou, Xiamen and other places. The price of the telegram, in addition to the cost of the line, must be increased by one-half of the water line cost, and the cost of the telegram is actually half more expensive than that of the Chinese Telegraph Office. Moreover, the direct line from Shanghai to Fuzhou of the Chinese Telegraph Office is exceptionally smooth since the major repairs. All telegrams sent to Fuzhou, Xiamen, Xiantou, Quanzhou, Guangzhou and various parts of Guangdong cost only one dime per word for clear text and Chinese, and only two dimes per word for secret text and foreign languages.

Fighting Over Reed Mats Results in Death

The Kaiping Bureau in Pudong has the Ganfu steamer. It loaded flour the night before, and Xiao Wuzi, a laborer from Jiangbei, Zhang Dayizi, 45 years old, were all working. Because of the heavy rain, they stopped working and slept at the bow of the ship. They clashed over a reed mat, pulling, twisting, pushing, and hitting each other. Zhang Dayizi fell to the ground unconscious. Colleagues tried to rescue him, but he did not breathe and died on the ship. The water patrol police station arrested Tian and sent Zhang's body to the Lifesaving Bureau for an autopsy. Yesterday, Tian was escorted to the court for autopsy.

Continued Report on the Martial Arts Drama in Front of Gaochang Temple

Guowen News Agency reported that after the clash between the workers of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant and the ticket seller of the China Merchants Tram Company in front of Gaochang Temple, the fourth and first tram lines stopped at the South Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road. As of yesterday, they had not resumed. The injured people in the hospital have not changed, and their lives are expected to be saved. As of yesterday, the China Merchants Tram Company had sent an official letter to Chen Shaokuan, the director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, and the tram association proposed four requests to the company in the afternoon. The Jiangnan Shipyard Labor Union also issued a declaration. However, it was heard that Lu Bohong said that the negotiations on transportation were two different things. What should be negotiated should be negotiated, and the traffic from the station to Gaochang Temple should also be requested by the labor union to resume first. Yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched inspectors to investigate the scene of the incident and ordered the trams to resume operations first. Chen Shaokuan is scheduled to come to Shanghai today and tomorrow, and he should be able to handle it properly.

Another Accomplice in the Xinxin Embezzlement Case is Apprehended

▲ Bian Chansheng Left Without Saying Goodbye

▲ Apprehended From His Hometown and Escorted to Shanghai

When the Xinxin Company's textiles department experienced a turmoil in the past, employees colluded with each other to embezzle more than 180,000 yuan. It was not discovered until last winter. The embezzling employees had successively resigned, leaving only one person. He voluntarily surrendered, and the case of embezzling a large amount of money was exposed. Detective Wang Changgen arrested several people and sent them to the Special District Local Court, which sentenced them to imprisonment. The company took into account the remorse of the one who surrendered and gave him a chance to start anew and did not pursue the matter. The police station stipulated in a special article that the leniency of surrender could not exempt him from all criminal penalties, so he was still prosecuted according to law and was also convicted, but he was sentenced to a lenient suspended sentence. When that person surrendered and reported the crime, Bian Chansheng, an employee of the textiles department from Qingshan, Huzhou, suddenly abandoned his job and fled. The company initially thought that he was also a member of the embezzlement group. When the Zhang and other four people were arrested, they confessed that Bian was indeed an accomplice. The Laozha Police Station sent detectives Liu Junqing and Wang Yingjie to Bian's hometown to arrest him and escort him to Shanghai. He was sent to the Special Court yesterday, but he denied participating in the fraud, saying that he had been working in the textiles department since the opening of Xinxin, and resigned and returned to his hometown on December 17 last year. However, according to Li Minzhou, the manager of the company, the defendant left without saying goodbye and had not gone through the resignation approval procedures. Judge Zhou ordered the defendant to be detained and questioned again on Saturday.

A Libertine

▲ Died of Syphilis

Li Yuyi, an employee of a silversmith shop at No. 339 Shanhai Pass Road, was only 27 years old. He liked to engage in promiscuous activities and often went on clandestine tours outside of work. As a result, he contracted syphilis, which gradually worsened. On New Year's Day of the Gregorian calendar, taking advantage of the work stoppage, he went to a hospital in Ximen for treatment, but the poison had entered his bones and was incurable. The morning before yesterday, he took a rickshaw back to the shop, and as he was about to arrive, he fell backward in the rickshaw, his eyes closed, and his face suddenly changed. The police officer at post No. 1665 saw him on the way and stopped the rickshaw. After questioning the rickshaw driver, he immediately ordered him to be sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he was already dead. The police officer reported to the police station and ordered him to be sent to the Fielun Road autopsy site. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo of the Special Court came to the site to conduct an autopsy. After the police station summoned his cousin Li Liangyu to the case for questioning, he ordered Li to issue a certificate to claim the body for coffin and burial.

The Shanghai Xinzhong Engineering Co., Ltd. held its fourth regular shareholders' meeting at 3 pm yesterday at the company's office at No. 47 Ningbo Road. He reported on the company's situation last year. Then, Manager Zhi Bingyuan reported that the total turnover exceeded the previous year's results. The black oil engine was the best product produced. More than 1,000 horsepower were sold in one year. The largest engine produced had 80 horsepower. It is currently working on the production of a four-stroke 90 horsepower engine and expanding the electrical machinery manufacturing department to manufacture AC generators to meet the needs of domestic lighting plants. After reporting on the accounts and the balance sheet, the auditor Chen Ruhong verified that the accounts were correct and immediately passed the profit distribution plan, with an official interest of 8% and a bonus of 4.5%. It was also passed as proposed. Next, supervisors were elected. Xie Chunpu and Xu Enzeng were re-elected. Finally, it was resolved to increase the capital by 100,000 yuan to expand the company. The meeting adjourned at 6 o'clock.

Qin Bowei Publishes Predictions for This Spring's Epidemic

Qin Bowei, the standing committee member of the National Medical Association, practices medicine in Shangwen Road, Xiaoximen. Based on his experience of celestial time, luck, and experience, he published an article predicting this spring's epidemic, which is thousands of words. The following is excerpted for the citizens' information: "The winter was severely cold, and there was a large amount of snowfall after the beginning of spring. The cold and dry air is very pervasive. According to the ancient theory of luck, it is appropriate for fire and heat to be used. Therefore, the disease this spring should be dominated by lung diseases. The most common is dry cough, followed by sore throat. Cooling and clearing should be used for both. The influenza symptoms, initially seeing fear of cold, headache, desire to cough, limb weakness, stiff neck, and red urine, are especially prone to stagnation and heat, making people confused. At the beginning, sweating too much is not allowed, and in the middle, cooling and moisturizing too much is not allowed. Nowadays, many people mistakenly think that headache and stiff neck are what Western medicine calls spinal meningitis, but it is similar but not the same."

The Ship Collision Case Has Been Resolved

On January 2 this year, He Jinsheng's ship collided with the Northern Navigation Company's Beifu vessel near the Dalai Wharf in Huangpu. He Jinsheng's cargo was immediately sunk at the time, and a crew member, Wu Laohu, was drowned. After several negotiations and mediation by the Shanghai County Government, an agreement was reached yesterday. As a result, the Beifu vessel decided to pay He Jinsheng 1,000 yuan for the damaged cargo, and 300 yuan to the family of Wu Laohu, who was drowned. The district chief and township chief concerned agreed on the spot, and with the permission of the Shanghai County Government, both parties signed a certificate. The case has been completely closed.

Shanghai News: Annual Shareholders' Meeting of the Bank of East Asia

▲ Zhou Shouchen Reports on Progress

On February 22nd, at 3:00 PM, the Bank of East Asia in Hong Kong held its annual shareholders' meeting at its office. Attendees included Chairman of the Board Zhou Shouchen, directors Feng Pingshan, Li Guanchun, Huang Runtang, Jian Yingfu, Guo Youting, Chen Chengshi, Huang Zhuchen, shareholder and General Manager Jian Dongpu, Manager Li Zifang, shareholders Guo Shaojian, Pan Xiaochu, Tan Yashi, Li Lansheng, Zhou Shinan, and others. Chairman Zhou Shouchen reported on the business situation, stating: "Esteemed shareholders, today is the date of the annual shareholders' meeting of this bank. I am very pleased to gather with you all once again. The financial statements for 1930, along with the reports from the Board of Directors and auditors, have been duly attached and submitted. I trust you will examine them thoroughly. Following the Hong Kong custom, I will simply read them aloud and refrain from further elaboration. The financial statements for 1930, combined with the 447,994.65 yuan carried over from the previous year, show a net profit of 1,456,425.01 yuan. Recalling last year, business was sluggish not only in Guangdong and Hong Kong but also worldwide. Yet, this bank still achieved this result, which I believe will satisfy all shareholders and is cause for celebration for the bank's future. Examining the business situation of the past year, the bank's deposits, mortgages, and remittances have all increased. Due to the increase in deposit income, the head office and branches have vigorously promoted mortgage business. The Board of Directors has reviewed the mortgage collateral and considers it to be very secure. The bank's decorations, furniture, and miscellaneous items were previously written down to one yuan. Last year, all expenses for decorations and furniture were accounted for as expenses, so no further funds need to be spent on decorations and furniture in the future. To strengthen the foundation of the bank, the Board of Directors proposes to allocate 500,000 yuan from last year's profits to the surplus reserve. Combined with the 1.75 million yuan from the previous year, this totals 2.25 million yuan, accounting for 45% of the capital. The Board of Directors believes that increasing the surplus reserve is a very good measure, and I trust you will agree. The Board of Directors proposes to pay a dividend of six yuan per share and a bonus of two yuan per share for 1930, the same as the previous year. During this time of global difficulty, the bank's business has achieved these results thanks to the diligence and dedication of our managers and staff. The Board of Directors is very grateful. However, we have noticed that the cost of living has been rising, so we have allocated an extra bonus from last year's profits to give to all staff members as a salary increase to encourage them. I trust you will all support this. Besides what I have mentioned above, there is nothing else to report. I propose that this annual report be approved. Now that this motion has been seconded, if anyone has any questions, I will gladly answer them."

"Singing Girl Red Peony" Previewed at the Guanglu Theater Yesterday

"Singing Girl Red Peony," China's first full-dialogue and singing film, produced by the Minzhong National Film Company, filmed by the Star Film Company, and recorded by Pathe Records, took six months and cost 120,000 yuan. It has now been completed. Yesterday, at 10:00 AM, a special preview was held at the Guanglu Theater on Museum Road. Over 600 people attended with invitations, including members of the press, the film industry, various celebrities, and representatives from Paramount, Fox, and other companies stationed in Shanghai. First, Ju Jianyun took the stage to report on the film's production and sound recording process, bringing together talent from both Star and Pathe companies. After much research and effort, the sound recording was scrapped four times before succeeding on the fifth attempt. The difficulty of the work and the spirit of meticulousness can be imagined. The screening began at 10:30 AM. The film is 13,000 feet long and divided into 18 reels. Those in attendance expressed great satisfaction with the film's moving plot, profound performances, clear sound, and excellent tone. Many female guests were moved to tears. The screening ended at 12:30 PM, and many Chinese and foreign guests shook hands with key Star employees to congratulate them on their success. Several first-run theaters in the city are competing for the right to premiere the film, and a decision will be made within three days.

Automobile News

Essay

China's Road Administration Today and the Work of the Road Association

— Da Dao

—Report by Road Association Representative Mr. Ye Keliang at the American Road Builders' Association Convention—

The American Road Builders' Association held its 28th annual convention in St. Louis from January 10th to 16th this year. The local Road Association was invited to send a representative to participate. Wang Zhengting, the president of the Road Association, telegraphed Ye Keliang, the Consul General stationed in Chicago, to represent the association. Yesterday, Mr. Ye reported on the convention's proceedings and sent over 40 types of brochures describing road construction equipment. The translated excerpts of the representative's speech are as follows for the reference of those concerned with road administration. Details of the meeting will be translated continuously. Mr. Ye's speech mentioned that he represents the Chinese government and the National Roads Construction Association of China and extends sincere greetings to all members and representatives of the Association. The improvement of China's roads is a prerequisite for the national construction plan of the National Government. Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the leader of the Chinese Revolution, stipulated in his outline of national construction that one million miles of crushed stone roads must be built throughout the country. At present, the foundation of our country's government is becoming more stable. We are adopting new methods to strive for the construction of a new China, which is easier than in the past.

On May 23, 1929, the National Design Committee, presided over by the Ministry of Railways, held a meeting in Nanjing that lasted for about three months. It completed various important plans for road construction. The designated national road system is divided into two major parts: the headquarters and border defense, with a total of twelve trunk lines to be completed in four phases. This is truly good news for the construction of a new China. However, due to the initial stabilization of the overall situation and a shortage of funds, while road construction cannot be delayed, it was decided to build dirt roads first and then gradually improve them. In recent years, the road-building movement has been booming throughout the country. The headquarters routes have been opened to traffic in sections, which shows that our country is now striving to promote this transportation in order to fully develop the transportation industry. Since the abolition of the likin tax, the new tax rates adopted by our country recently have greatly benefited this. The gasoline tax has been reduced from 1.75% to 1.70% per box, and the kerosene tax has also been reduced. Only the petroleum tax has been slightly increased. The road construction machinery tax has also been reduced from 10% to 7.5%, and the agricultural machinery tax has been reduced from 10% to 5%. Only the automobile tax has been increased from 22.5% to 30%, and the truck tax has been increased from 12.5% to 20%.

The Road Association is a committee of the Pan-Pacific Association. The chairman is Dr. Wang Zhengting, the current Minister of Foreign Affairs and President of the Road Association. After the dissolution of the wife committee, the Road Association was formed to replace it. The association is engaged in road construction propaganda, which has attracted the attention of the whole country. It publishes the Road Monthly, the Road Encyclopedia, and other books on road engineering, plans the national automobile road network, investigates the transportation situation in various provinces, introduces road engineering specialists, purchases road construction machinery, answers road market inquiries, and encourages members' enthusiasm for road construction. It also establishes branches in various provinces and regions, all to the extent of its capabilities, in order to complete the great cause of building roads throughout the country. The association has been established for ten years and its efforts have paid off considerably. The newly built roads amount to more than 100,000 li. In most cities, the city walls have been demolished and replaced with tree-lined streets. In the northwestern provinces, the association's chief executive, Wu Shan, earnestly joined in the construction of large mountain roads, opening up the millennia-old dangerous Xiaohan passage and building a 1,700-li automobile road connecting Henan, Shaanxi, and Gansu, with a width of 60 feet. The journey that used to take months can now be completed in just a few days. The association also plans to open a road engineering specialty school and a road market model library exhibition hall. Currently, to celebrate its 10th anniversary, it has announced that it will hold a road market exhibition in Shanghai in April this year, soliciting various road administration-related machinery, charts, models, specimens, etc. for display to the people of the country in order to promote the improvement of road market policies.

Last November, the association asked the National Government to issue a nationwide order for the regular troops to participate in the construction of national roads in order to realize the purpose of turning soldiers into workers and to ensure the early success of the roads that crisscross the country. In short, China's road construction does not lack manpower. Whenever needed, people arrive immediately. Guizhou, a poor province in China, felt the need to build roads, so the provincial authorities started work with 200,000 people. In just one winter, they built

Chevrolet's New Car with Many Styles

— Ying

▲ Nine Types of Car Bodies ▲ Wheelbase Two Inches Wider Than Old Cars

This publication has already published articles on new cars from various manufacturers, so there is no need to repeat them. However, the Chevrolet 1931 new car has been released recently, and the variety of car body styles and the excellent internal structure are even better than the others. Therefore, the various advantages are described in detail to the readers as follows.

▲ High Reputation: The Chevrolet 1931 new car has nine different car body styles. This time, automobile exhibitions have been held one after another in various parts of the United States. Guests who saw the many Chevrolet new cars praised them and were praised for two months. The wheelbase of various new cars is two inches wider than the old cars, and the width of the car room is also better than the old cars. As for the beauty of the appearance and the elegance of the paint, they are even more minor matters. The two-inch wider wheelbase makes the car wheels one inch and nine inches long, which greatly improves the safety of passengers when driving. The new fish-shaped car body is wider in all parts, but the top is lower. In terms of appearance, the lines are reduced, and the front is painted with a crest pattern, which is particularly unique. The lowering of the driver's seat makes it easier to see when driving and makes the front crossbar parallel to the windshield. In this way, the windshield can also increase safety and is not easy to break.

▲ Complete Accessories: The side panels are also longer than the old cars, but the front is much narrower. The back is constructed using a new method. The storage tank is placed at the back and is not exposed at all. As for the car doors, they can be closed by hand, regardless of whether they are front or rear. All kinds of new cars have new car door devices. As for the inside of the car room, all kinds of accessories are available. Such as cigarette ash boxes, armrests, pure silk curtains, etc., are particularly characteristic. All doors and windows are automatically closed. The rear of the touring car is wide. When the car tent is folded, it is just in the place of the rear seat, which is very convenient because there is no glass window. In terms of the mechanical structure, the improvements are particularly outstanding. Such as the division of the car room, the convenience of driving, the durability of the meshing parts, and the convenience of the transmission function are all unique to ordinary vehicles. There are four hydraulic shock absorbers, and there are four-wheel brakes. In addition to various touring special heat reducers, there are also lead objects covering them. Steel wire wheels and hub caps are also made of aluminum, as are the front and rear car lights. Therefore, the device of the new car is quite complete.

▲ Enlarged Car Top: The car top of the new car is also longer than the old car. The highest point is like a crown. The front railing is larger, and the rods in the railing are made of metal. The semicircular shape connects the railings one by one. The horn is installed on the front, just below the left car light, and the power of the heat reducer is particularly strong. The driving wheel has three spokes, while the old car has four. In terms of ratio, the new car is from twelve to one, while the old car is from nine and five to one. The six-cylinder new car has a horsepower of up to 50 horsepower. The piston installed in the front engine is based on the one invented in 1928 and modified. Therefore, it is both glossy and durable. The crank rod is also stronger than in the past. A rubber boot is placed on top of the carburetor and accelerator. In this way, even in cold weather, the water will not freeze, and the transmission function is also quite powerful. There is really nothing that is not perfect.

News

Harbin Limits the Number of Passengers in Cars

— Che

Harbin is a key point of the China Eastern Railway and an important town in Jiang Province. Therefore, the population is very dense and commerce is prosperous. The road construction is no less than that of Beijing and Shanghai. The traffic of cars is naturally convenient, but the restriction on the number of passengers carried by cars is quite strict. The special police department is deeply aware that the arbitrary carrying of passengers by cars is a source of danger and must be banned. Therefore, at the end of last month, it issued an order to the Great Automobile Association, stating that Article 88 of the regulations of the municipal traffic management department stipulates that large cars are limited to carrying 15 people in winter and spring and 17 people in summer and autumn, excluding the driver and ticket seller. If it is a Ford card, it is only allowed to carry 14 people in winter and spring and 16 people in summer and autumn. It has long been submitted for publication and has been implemented for a long time. However, in the winter of the 18th year, the Harbin Great Automobile Association reported that during the military period, many soldiers rode without tickets. In addition, staff from various agencies were exempt from tickets, which led to a sharp reduction in income for each car and requested an increase of two seats. This department gave special approval to show expediency. It is currently found that the military period is long gone, and the free ticket vouchers for staff from various agencies have also been stopped. The original reason for increasing the number of seats does not exist at this time. Moreover, large cars carrying passengers beyond the number stipulated in the regulations exceed the weight limit, which is most likely to cause danger. As far away as the tragic train accident at Bazhan and as close as the cases of Nos. 541, 579, and 488 large cars hitting pedestrians, although the cause of the accident was the driver's negligence, the main reason was that too many passengers were carried, making it impossible to move freely. The volume of large cars is limited, and too many passengers are crowded, which not only hinders public health but also provides opportunities for thieves to commit crimes. There are countless drawbacks. In order to maintain public order and prevent danger, this department must restore the original regulations on the number of seats carried by large cars.

▲The Liyang Tong He Rui Tang Eye Medicine Branch announces: Our branch is located at number two, lane two, Yanqing Lane, Xiamen Road, in the British Concession. We meticulously produce two types of clam shell eye medicine, red and white. We produce over twenty thousand units annually and are a long-standing supplier to major Shanghai philanthropists for distribution. The effects are remarkably swift and widely praised. Furthermore, Zhu Huang Ju Guang San (Pearl Yellow Light Gathering Powder) and Baobao Mo Yi Wan (Eight Treasure Mo Yi Pill) are said to be especially effective for all dangerous eye diseases.
